The Shanghai-Wuxi Highway is Scheduled to Open on the 16th 93

Postal Contract to be Established Within Days

The Shanghai-Wuxi Highway has been fully completed and is scheduled to hold an opening ceremony in Nanxiang on the 15th of this month and officially open to traffic on the 16th. The reporter of Huadong News Agency details the situation as follows.

Postal Contract to be Established Within Days

After the Shanghai-Wuxi Highway is opened to traffic, transportation in Changshu and Taicang will be very convenient. Shanghai mail is usually transported by the Beijing-Shanghai train and inland transport ships, which takes a long time and is very inconvenient. Now, in order to facilitate the mailing of letters and packages from Jiading, Taicang, Changshu and other places, the post office specifically contacted the long-distance bus company yesterday and reached a postal transport contract. It is very satisfactory and will be signed and established within days.

Twenty Round Trips Per Day

The company has a total of 65 cars, each of which can accommodate 25 passengers. There are 20 round trips per day. The road between Wuxi and Shanghai is 140 kilometers long, and the travel time is 3 hours and 30 minutes. The distance from Shanghai to Changshu is 95 kilometers, and the travel time is 2 hours and 30 minutes. The distance to Taicang is 40 kilometers, and the travel time is 1 hour. The company is also offering passenger discounts during the opening period of three months, and the ticket price will be calculated at 20% off. The company also stipulates: (1) The fare is set at slightly less than 3 cents per kilometer in silver dollars, and a temporary 20% discount is listed at the beginning of the opening. (2) Where there are no stations along the route, they will be added at any time as necessary, in order to facilitate passengers. (3) Passengers are allowed 15 kilograms of free luggage. Those over 15 kilograms will be charged one-eighth of the ticket price per 10 kilograms. (4) A fraction of 5 "li" for half the ticket price is counted as 1 "fen."

Full Line and Branch Line Passenger Ticket Prices

The passenger ticket prices for the Shanghai-Wuxi long-distance buses have been set as follows: From Wuxi to Dongting, 14 cents; to Anzhen, 42 cents; to Yangjiatian, 62 cents; to Wengjiazhuang, 72 cents; to Liantangzhen, 82 cents; to Changshu, 1 yuan and 8 cents; to Guli Village, 1 yuan and 36 cents; to Baimaotzhen, 1 yuan and 54 cents; to Zhitang, 1 yuan and 68 cents; to Mizhen, 1 yuan and 79 cents; to Zhitang, 1 yuan and 88 cents; to Shuangfeng, 1 yuan and 97 cents; to Maojia Guanyintang, 2 yuan and 6 cents; to Taicang, 2 yuan and 21 cents; to Xinfengzhen, 2 yuan and 34 cents; to Gelongzhen, 2 yuan and 40 cents; to Waigang, 2 yuan and 48 cents; to Jiading, 2 yuan and 66 cents; to Malu, 2 yuan and 80 cents; to Nanxiang, 2 yuan and 93 cents; to Luoyangqiao, 3 yuan and 12 cents; to Shanghai, 3 yuan and 36 cents. The branch line from Changshu to Suzhou is calculated as follows: From Changshu to Yingcheng, 11 cents; to Xinzhuang, 24 cents; to Wuta, 33 cents; to Weijingtang, 46 cents; to Koutou, 62 cents; to Lumu, 70 cents; to Suzhou, 78 cents.

Regulations for Recruiting Merchant Agents for China Merchants

The regulations for recruiting merchant agents for the Shanghai-Wuxi Long-Distance Bus Company are as follows: 1. In order to facilitate passengers, the Company has specifically set up agency stations in small towns along the route to provide passengers with stations for getting on and off. The Company recruits local merchants to act as agents. 2. Any store or household living on both sides of the route through which the Company's buses pass who is willing to act as an agent may do so as long as it meets the requirements of these Regulations. 3. If there are more than two people who wish to act as agents in each location, the Company has the right to select and designate them. 4. Anyone who wishes to act as an agent must fill out a voluntary application and find a reputable merchant in the local area or county seat to guarantee everything. They must also pay a deposit of 50 yuan in silver to the Company (this deposit does not accrue interest). If business is booming in the future and the Company deems it necessary to increase the deposit, it shall be complied with. 5. If the agent is a local government agency or organization, it shall appoint a person in charge to handle the business. 6. The agency station established by the agent should have a waiting room large enough to accommodate more than ten people, and must be equipped with tables and chairs for passengers to sit and wait for the bus. 7. The passenger tickets sold at the agency station should be obtained in advance from the Company's designated self-operated station. When the tickets are about to run out, preparations should be made to continue to receive them. However, the amount of tickets received shall not exceed 80% of the amount of the deposit paid. Under no circumstances may the agent print and replace them without permission. Violators will be immediately dismissed. 8. The agent shall fill in the number of passenger tickets sold and the amount of ticket fares in the Company's daily payment report every day, and submit them together with the ticket money to the first bus the next morning. If the payment is delayed by more than one day, 1/10 of the monthly agency fee will be deducted. 9. The agent shall sell tickets daily in the order of the ticket numbers and report the full amount daily. It is not allowed to sell tickets from the middle or sell tickets in reverse order, or report smaller numbers than the actual numbers. If there is any failure to sell in order, intercept and leave ticket money unresolved, the full monthly agency fee for that month will be cancelled. If the circumstances are serious, the agency right will be revoked. 10. When the bus arrives, the agent should collect tickets from passengers. If passengers have not purchased tickets or are riding past the stop, they should be ordered to make up the ticket and hand over the ticket after punching it. The collected waste tickets shall be sorted, numbered, and sealed separately for each station on a daily basis, and submitted together with the daily report to the ticket office. If ten or more are found missing in the whole month, a demerit will be recorded. If waste tickets are fraudulently resold, in addition to ordering compensation and revoking the agency right, the case will be sent to the local government agency to recover the losses in accordance with the seriousness of the circumstances. 10. In addition to the seals and ticket punching copper seals, etc., that the agent station should use, it may receive them from the Company. All other stationery that should be used must be provided by itself, but it may be entrusted to the Company for the price to be processed, in order to be uniform. 12. The agent station's housing, as well as all miscellaneous expenses, advertising, and business expenses, shall be borne by itself, and the Company shall not be responsible for it. 13. At the end of each month, the Company will deduct 10% of the total amount of passenger tickets sold at the station as remuneration. However, when it exceeds 200 yuan, for every 100 yuan increase, the increased remuneration fee will be reduced by 1/10. For example, for 300 yuan, the increased remuneration fee of more than 100 yuan is 9 yuan, and for 400 yuan, the remuneration fee of more than 300 yuan is 8 yuan, and the total is 37 yuan (and so on). The agency station's remuneration fee will be issued by the Company on a regular basis after the monthly settlement and shall not be intercepted by itself from the ticket money. 14. The agent shall strictly abide by the Company's various rules and regulations and must obey all announcements of the Company and accept the inspection and guidance of the Company's station managers and inspectors. 15. The agent shall not engage in any acts such as overcharging for tickets, fraud, or embezzlement, or allow relatives, friends, or passengers to ride without a ticket. Otherwise, once it is found out, the loss suffered by the Company as a result shall be compensated, and the local judicial authority shall be requested to punish it in accordance with the seriousness of the circumstances. 16. If the agent does not wish to continue to act as an agent, it shall report to the Company one month in advance, and shall be allowed to resign after finding a successor. 17. If necessary, the Company may take it back at any time for self-management, and the agent shall not make any requests because of this. 18. If the agent has any business matters to contact, it shall obtain the approval of the Company or the person in charge of each station in advance and be given a ride voucher before being allowed to ride for free. Otherwise, a full ticket must be purchased. 19. When all agency stations pay the ticket money to the driver, the driver shall sign and save the stub of the payment book for future reference. The accounting department shall issue a receipt as proof of receiving the money. If there is any unclear handover and loss as a result, the agency station shall still be responsible. 20. The entry and exit of silver prices must comply with the Company's announced water table, and no high or low prices or arbitrary pricing shall be allowed. 21. The Company shall not be responsible for all external behaviors and monetary disputes of the agent. 22. If there are any shortcomings in these regulations, the Company may amend them at any time.

Singapore Chinese Chamber of Commerce Requests the Opening of a Nanyang Shipping Route 94

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company is currently planning to proceed.

The Da Gong She reports that the Singapore Chinese Chamber of Commerce believes that Singapore is an important metropolis in Nanyang, with over ten thousand overseas Chinese residing there. Since the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-1895, the shipping routes to the area have been interrupted, leading to difficulties in the transportation of domestic goods and severely impacting sales. In recent years, domestic products have been almost entirely displaced by foreign goods, which is deeply lamented. To promote domestic goods, the Chamber sent representatives back to China in November of last year to collect samples of domestic goods from various regions, which was well-received by the overseas Chinese community. The Chamber has scheduled a domestic goods exhibition to be held in Singapore on October 15th of this year and has sent letters to domestic goods organizations in various regions, encouraging manufacturers to participate enthusiastically. As the opening of the exhibition is fast approaching, the Chamber still faces difficulties in transportation. To ensure the success of domestic goods in overseas markets, it is necessary to first establish shipping routes to maintain long-term development. Therefore, the Chamber sent a telegram to the Ministry of Communications in March of this year, requesting them to instruct the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to purchase additional ships and extend the company's Hong Kong route to Singapore to facilitate the promotion of domestic goods. However, as this has not yet been realized, the Chamber sent letters to various business organizations in this city yesterday, requesting unified support to urge the authorities to implement this plan as soon as possible. The Da Gong She reporter inquired with the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company yesterday and learned that the company has already planned to open a shipping route to Nanyang. However, the leasing of wharves in various Nanyang ports and the purchase of additional ships have not yet been finalized, and due to economic considerations, it is difficult to open the route in the short term.

Eurasia Aviation Corporation Successfully Completes Test Flight of the Shaanxi-Chengdu Route; Opening Date to Be Determined After the Aircraft Returns to Shanghai; Li Jingcong Returned to Shanghai Yesterday Morning and Telegraphed a Report to Beijing 95

The Eurasia Aviation Corporation, under the orders of the Ministry of Communications to open a new Shaanxi-Chengdu route, dispatched a Junkers No. 6 aircraft, which took off from Longhua Airport in Shanghai the day before yesterday. It arrived in Xi'an at 4:31 PM that day. At 8:40 AM yesterday morning, the aircraft, with three people on board—acting head of the flight group He En'er, Xi'an station chief Yang Xingzhong, and German pilot Kast—took off from Xi'an station to test the new Shaanxi-Chengdu route. It arrived safely in Chengdu at 12:27 PM that afternoon, landing at the airport. The aircraft did not stop when passing through Nanzheng (i.e., Hanzhong). Although the direct route is 600 kilometers, the flight speed was particularly reduced due to the numerous mountains and ridges. The inspection of the mountains along the way yielded excellent results. It is expected that the flight will take approximately two hours when the route is officially opened. The aircraft is scheduled to fly from Chengdu to Xi'an on the 4th, and then return to Shanghai via Zhengzhou and Nanjing, following the Shanghai-Xinjiang route, before officially opening the route. After General Manager Li Jingcong arrived in Shanghai from Beijing yesterday morning, he received a report that the test flight was successful and immediately telegraphed the Ministry of Communications in Beijing. The opening date and ticket prices will be determined after the aircraft returns to Shanghai. It is expected that the route will be officially opened before the end of August.

Stock Exchange: A Humorous Official Letter 96

Forwarding Tax Payment to the Public Works Department to Inquire Whether the Department Accepts

The Chinese Ratepayers' Association sent a letter to the Director-General of the Shanghai Municipal Council of the International Settlement, stating: "Sir, according to a letter from the Shanghai Chinese Stock Exchange, 'Our tenant, the Guoxin Bank, claims that the Public Works Department arbitrarily overestimated the property value, considering that the rent of 800 yuan is definitely not the correct amount, which has caused complications in the collection of property tax. In fact, based on the current market conditions, a monthly rent of 800 yuan is already quite high. Now, the bank requests your association to uphold justice and provide assistance, and asks our exchange to provide proof, etc. After investigation, the bank's rent is indeed 800 yuan per month, with a contract, rent receipt, and account books as proof. Previously, because the building was vacant and no one was managing it, it had been empty for more than two years. Therefore, in March of this year, we rented it to the bank, reducing the rent to be better than leaving it empty for a long time. In this time of economic depression, we naturally cannot take costs into account. This is the situation of our exchange renting the property to the bank. If the Public Works Department, under the current circumstances, truly wishes to assume that the bank's annual rent is 17,000 yuan and deems it appropriate, then our exchange would be delighted to allow the Guoxin Bank to terminate the lease. Please have the department come to rent the property directly or find a tenant on our behalf, and we are willing to offer 5% as a commission. Our exchange's stock exchange building has many vacant rooms, and we would also like the department to quickly rent them or find tenants based on the valuation ratio of the Guoxin Bank, in order to increase the rent and avoid the pain of prolonged vacancy. This would greatly benefit property owners throughout Shanghai; otherwise, property owners will only suffer the blame of tenants, and tenants will also suffer the department's exploitation. We are specially writing to verify; we hope your esteemed association will investigate and handle it.' The above information was received by the association. After investigation, the agent lawyer of Guoxin Bank has already sent a letter to your esteemed department regarding this case. Now that there is proof from the landlord, your esteemed department should believe that the reported actual rent is reliable. If your esteemed department insists that the rent is definitely not just 800 yuan per month, then does your esteemed department have the ability to accept the exchange's opinion, according to the information in the letter? We are writing to request your investigation and joint handling." To Mr. Fei, Acting Director-General of the Shanghai Municipal Council of the International Settlement.

Tax-Free Export Goods from Shanghai: Customs Exempts Dredging Surcharge for One Year

Jianghai Customs Notice for General Information 100

Tang Haian, Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs, and Luo Fu De, Customs Commissioner, issued Joint Notice No. 1458 yesterday regarding the exemption of dredging surcharges for one year on tax-free export goods and re-export goods from Shanghai, stating: "Now, in accordance with the order of the Ministry of Finance, all tax-free export goods and re-export goods from Shanghai will be exempt from the dredging surcharge for one year starting from August 1st of this year. All merchants are hereby notified for general information. This notice is hereby issued."

City Chamber of Commerce Notifies All Industries That Changes in Directors and Supervisors of Companies Must Be Registered 102

The Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce yesterday notified all industry trade associations, stating: "Sir, on the 29th of this month, we received Instruction No. 6441 from the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, which stated: 'In accordance with Instruction No. 35936 from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, the names of the directors and supervisors of a company are among the items that must be registered for the company. Re-election upon the expiration of terms or supplementary elections to fill vacancies constitute changes in the registered items and must be reported for registration of the changes in accordance with the law. We have previously notified you to comply with this requirement. Currently, many companies in various regions still disregard the law and delay reporting re-elections or supplementary elections. This is inappropriate. Hereafter, the competent authorities in various regions should pay attention to the companies within their jurisdiction that have already been registered. If there are directors or supervisors who have been re-elected or vacancies that have not been reported, they should be ordered to report the changes for registration in accordance with the law to comply with the regulations. In addition to separate orders, this order is hereby issued for your bureau's compliance,' etc. In addition to paying attention to compliance at all times, this order is hereby issued for your association's information, and for you to notify all members to inform all companies to take note," etc. Accordingly, this order is recorded and forwarded for your information and for you to notify your affiliated industries to comply as required.

Approved Amendments to the Articles of Association and Submitted Them to the Ministry of Finance for Approval

City Chamber of Commerce Cables Shaanxi Provincial Government, etc., Requesting Reduction of Special Tax on Domestic Enamelware 104

The Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce cabled the Shaanxi Provincial Government and the Office of the Financial Commissioner yesterday, stating: "(Titles omitted) On the 31st of this month, we received a letter from the Enamelware Trade Association, stating that the members of the association, such as the Zhonghua Enamel Factory, proposed that enamelware has long been popular throughout the country. In order to maintain the national foundation, the government has spared no effort in protecting and promoting the budding domestic industry. The taxes and levies imposed on it have always been in accordance with the Ministry's regulations on machine-made domestic goods, which exempt it from repeated taxation in any region within the country except for the export tariff. However, in recent years, various provinces have unilaterally promulgated tax laws due to financial difficulties. Some provinces define it as a local specialty, while others define it as a consumer good. The names are different, and the tax rates vary, but none is heavier than the tax rate set by the Shaanxi Special Tax Bureau. The tax rate in Shaanxi is determined by the Office of the Financial Commissioner and is purely a unilateral law of one province. For enamelware items such as rice bowls and lunch boxes, the tax is almost 10% of the value, which merchants cannot afford. Moreover, Shaanxi is located deep in the northwest provinces. Once this heavy tax is imposed, not only will sales in the province be greatly reduced, but it will also be difficult to purchase from Shaanxi to other provinces. If we do not list the difficulties and request the Shaanxi authorities to review and amend them, the future of domestic goods will be greatly affected, and foreign goods may take the opportunity to enter. The Shaanxi authorities have always been enthusiastic about domestic goods and will certainly understand the government's painstaking efforts to protect them, consider the difficult situation of business, and make fair revisions. Please have the chamber send a letter to the City Chamber of Commerce for review and approval, and humbly request that you submit a document to the Shaanxi Provincial Financial Commissioner, requesting that the tax rate on enamelware items under the 'magnetic' category in the tax rate be revised and reduced as soon as possible to facilitate sales and maintain domestic production," etc., which was received by the chamber. It is appropriate to report this to your esteemed chamber for review and forwarding, which is truly a matter of public concern. The association stated that, according to past practice, goods treated according to the machine-made western-style goods tax law could circulate throughout the country after paying taxes at the first customs office in the place of origin. Apart from the Chongwenmen tax, no other taxes were levied. This method has been followed since the middle of the Qing Guangxu era until the Republic of China, even when the Likin tax had not yet been abolished. The enamelware of the member factories of the association is manufactured by Chinese factories and enjoys the treatment of the machine-made western-style goods tax law. After paying all the regular and additional taxes at the Shanghai Customs, it should not be taxed again when sold in your province according to the above-mentioned precedents. The factory takes into consideration that the northwest provinces are financially strained and are currently focusing on water control and road construction, with everything needing to be rebuilt. Therefore, it cannot be treated as a normal case and cannot dare to request exemption from repeated taxation. However, it hopes that the enlightened authorities in Shaanxi province will reduce the tax rate. As the factory considers the situation and acts reasonably, it is not forcing the impossible. Your province will surely consider the fundamental purpose of cooperation between officials and the people and maintain the sales of domestic products. Therefore, we are writing to inform you of the situation and earnestly request your approval. The Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce respectfully asks."

Shen Zhenhua, the Chief of Police, Encourages Smokers to Register 105

Since being ordered by the bureau on the 20th of last month to encourage smokers within his jurisdiction to register, Shen Zhenhua, the Chief of the Lao Beimen Police Station, has seen several people come to the station to register every day. However, there are still those who are hesitant to register. Now, in accordance with the bureau's orders, he has organized an encouragement team to conduct door-to-door encouragement within his jurisdiction starting today and to conduct investigations with various shops at any time in order to achieve twice the result with half the effort.

There are currently more than 32,000 overseas Chinese in the entire territory of Korea.

The Red Swastika Society Begs for Disaster Relief for Victims of the Yangtze River Provinces 110

The Southeast Main Society's Relief Team Has Arrived in Wuhan; Zhijiang County in Hubei Province Reports a Catastrophic Submergence

The Joint General Office of the Southeast Societies of the Red Swastika Society is actively preparing for the relief of the flood disaster in the Yangtze River provinces. The Nanjing Southeast Main Society has organized a team to go west to the most severely affected disaster area in that province to provide emergency relief, and has also sent telegrams to various societies and sectors, begging for disaster relief for the victims. At the same time, the society also received a report from Zhijiang County in Hubei Province on the catastrophic submergence, which is recorded in detail below.

The Nanjing Red Swastika Society's Circular Begging for Disaster Relief for the Victims stated: "Respectfully, Heaven has sent down a great disaster, and we have suffered a terrible flood. In the north, the Yellow River is overflowing, and the areas of Shandong, Henan, and Hebei have become half swamps. In the upper reaches, mountain torrents have erupted, and more than 100 counties in Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, and Anhui provinces have been flooded. According to telegrams received from various places, when the floodwaters suddenly arrived, the water level was as high as several or even more than ten zhang (a Chinese unit of length, approximately 3.3 meters or 10 feet). Dykes collapsed, and wherever the waves passed, cities and villages were turned into ruins in an instant. People were unable to escape and drowned in the raging waves. Counting the provinces together, there are millions of people. This is truly a disaster unseen in decades. Those who managed to escape are calling for help from rooftops, mountain peaks, or collapsed walls and withered trees. The situation is too tragic to bear. Even those who were fortunate enough to escape the floodwaters have had their houses, clothing, and food washed away, and they are exposed to the wind and rain, their lives hanging by a thread. These disaster victims are even more countless. Currently, the northern areas have been organized by the General Relief Society and the two Swastika Societies, in conjunction with various societies, to form a relief team and distribute relief in various directions. However, raising funds is difficult, and the work is very difficult. The relief team of this society has already set off for Hankou, carrying relief funds and medicines, and will transfer to the disaster area to carry out work. However, a cup of water compared to a cartload of firewood is shameful and cannot make up for the situation. The urgent task now is to combine the efforts of all and promote both righteous relief and official relief to save the people from their desperate situation and achieve stability. If we delay any longer, I fear that these millions of dying victims, the weak, will all starve to death, and the strong will take risks. What a tragic situation to imagine! At this time of successive years of famine and financial exhaustion, we know that fundraising is difficult. However, if we can all work together, accumulating grains can become a mountain. If we plan things with people in mind, we can surely turn the tide. All our compatriots, please have the compassion to treat others' hunger as your own and take universal actions to save everyone. The amount is not important, but at this time, every yuan can save a life. In this critical moment, please, gentlemen of virtue, act quickly! We bow to you for the sake of the millions of survivors. If you are willing to donate generously, please include the address and title of the letter with the donation and deliver it to No. 24 Xiaohuo Lane, Longwangmiao, or No. 4 Tongfu Lane, Juluda Road, Shanghai, or submit it to the collector. We will promptly issue a receipt, forward it to the disaster area, and publish it in the newspapers for acknowledgment to demonstrate our sincerity. Respectfully."

The Telegram from the Magistrate of Zhijiang County to the Red Swastika Society stated: "(Titles Omitted) The floods are overflowing, the land is submerged, and the disaster is catastrophic. Zhijiang County is the worst affected. On the 5th of this month, the water level of the Yangtze River suddenly exceeded the level of the past decade by two chi (Chinese foot, approximately 0.33 meters or 13 inches) or more. The Yangtze and Tuo Rivers overflowed, and the Ju and Zhang Rivers flowed wildly. In addition, with continuous wind and rain, mountain torrents erupted. Those near the river were spared, and those near the mountains could not protect themselves completely. The fields and crops were washed away, and the houses were turned into ruins. People and animals were swept away and became the spirits of the waves. Even those who were fortunate enough to survive are all hungry and exhausted, their faces pale and their bodies thin. They have not had a full meal for days. This time, the river suddenly rose, and the North Gate was breached. The residents were caught off guard and could only escape for their lives. Their properties were almost completely lost. The official embankment, which has been the first district's water conservancy project for hundreds of years without any changes, was also washed away by mountain floods, and the fields became wasteland. Yangxi is an important commercial town, but the backwater was too strong, and the houses were submerged to the roof, with nearly half of them collapsed. In Jiangbei (north of the river), the areas bordering the mountains and rivers, such as Changshoujing, Fuxingyuan, Sanheyuan, Yujiaxi Yuan, Wuliuyuan, Guojia Yuan, and the two towns of Jiangkou and Dongshi, are all threatened by the Yangtze River on the outside and washed by mountain floods on the inside. All of them have been breached. The Liumuyuan in the third district, the Xia Bailizhou, and the Gonghe Yuan are all on the Juyuzhang River basin. The mountain torrents flow from north to south, higher than the Yangtze River by more than a zhang. The force is even more fierce. Each Yuan has collapsed into a dyke, and the disaster is extremely severe. The houses and livestock have been damaged even more severely. The towns of Caopu and Fengtai have been completely destroyed. Shang Bailizhou, Yangjiaozhou, and Pianbaizhou, located between the Yangtze and Tuo Rivers, are attached to the outside of Shang Bailizhou, with a vast area. The Fufu Yuan, Fusheng Yuan, Tongfu, Tongde Yuan, and Xinli Yuan are surrounded by water on all sides and depend on the dyke for life. Fufu and Fusheng Yuan are low-lying, so they were the first to be breached. The dyke of Shang Bailizhou, which is closely connected to the two dykes, was also affected and suffered extremely severely. Attached to the outside of Yangjiaozhou are Zhonghe Yuan and Jicao Yuan. Zhonghe was breached, and Jicao followed. Jicao was breached, and Yangjiaozhou followed. Renhe Yuan, which is connected to Pianba, also suffered the disaster. Siyangzhou, Luzhou, Tongxinyuan, Zhongchengyuan, and Huazhouyuan are all south of the Nanhe River, located in the lower reaches of Songxi. Since the dike outside the North Gate of Songzi was breached, the water flow has been like a merchant building a bottle. None of the Yuan have survived. In short, most of the cities and towns in the county have been destroyed, and all the land for farming has been flattened. The disaster victims number about 100,000, and the losses amount to 50 million. Currently, the water level of the rivers is gradually receding, and it is possible to rush to plant autumn crops and autumn vegetables to try to make up for the losses. However, we are afraid that the river will flood again and that there is a lack of seeds. It is difficult to find a clean piece of land to escape to other places. If you step into the disaster area, you will see starving people on the road and hear crying that shakes the sky. It is truly unbearable to see or hear. I beg your esteemed society to show great compassion and provide prompt relief to save the people from the mud and water and relieve the suffering of the people. Let the dead be reborn and the scattered can reunite. The benevolence will be widespread and infinite. I respectfully report this to you and await your urgent instructions. Rao Guangya, Magistrate of Zhijiang County and Chairman of the Disaster Relief Committee, bows respectfully."

New System Implemented on the Shanghai-Yangzhou Route 111

Da Da and Da Tong Companies Cooperate to Eliminate Bad Practices Like Extortion for Liquor Tips

The privately-owned Da Da Steamboat Company and Da Tong Navigation Company, which operate the Shanghai-Yangzhou route on the lower reaches of the Yangtze River, have recently thoroughly reformed their ship operations for the convenience of merchants and travelers. As of yesterday, they abolished the compradore system on all ships and adopted a new management method. All the tea servers on board are now paid wages, eliminating the long-standing bad practice on Yangtze River ships of extorting tips for liquor and berth fees. Our reporter Lao Te from the New Sound News Agency visited Yang Guanbei, the manager of Da Da Company, who kindly explained in detail the cooperation between the two companies, the operational situation, and the actual progress of the improvements. These details are specially recorded below:

Cooperation Process

Mr. Yang first stated that our country's shipping industry has always lacked unity, and there are often internal conflicts among peers, resulting in losses for both sides. This is a major reason why Chinese merchant shipping cannot thrive. The Ministry of Transportation, recognizing this, promoted shipping cooperation in order to consolidate the foundation of the shipping industry. Da Da Company and Da Tong Company implemented cooperation in the 22nd year (of the Republic, i.e., 1933), establishing a joint office. They strive to reduce passenger and freight prices, with no intention of monopolizing. In recent years, rural bankruptcy and the nationwide economic downturn have led to a sharp decline in business compared to before. The two companies own a total of eight steamships, in addition to iron barges such as Chu Yuan and Chu Heng. In fact, supply already exceeds demand, and annual income and expenditure are barely enough to offset each other.

Actual Reform Situation

Director Peng of the Navigation Administration Bureau personally inspected and instructed on various points for improvement. Those that have been prepared include complying with the order to charge tea server liquor fees at a rate of 10% of the ticket price, and no overcharging is allowed, which has been implemented since August 1st. Awnings, handrails, and seats have been added separately. At the pier, police officers maintain order when ships arrive and depart. The pier management office also assigns 20 registered porters from each company to help passengers carry luggage and items, with fixed prices and no overcharging allowed. Since implementation, the order has been orderly, and there has been no crowding. Tea servers wear uniforms while serving, which is clean, tidy, and quite impressive. Each ship's cleaning duties are divided into sections and assigned to tea servers and sailors. In terms of life-saving equipment, there are multiple lifeboats, life jackets, and lifebuoys. Various medicines are also prepared to prevent emergencies. For fire prevention, there are pump machines and chemical fire extinguishers. Crew members and tea servers practice drills during their holidays to become proficient. There are also various books and magazines for passengers to read. After the ship sets sail, wireless radio is used to play elegant music and opera songs to entertain all the passengers' eyes and ears, relieving the boredom of the journey. Mr. Yang also said that Da Tong Company is now also complying with the order to make improvements, and the company's purpose is to serve the society, not just to make profits. Omissions and oversights are inevitable, and there will certainly be areas that are not perfect. We will study them carefully, and we also hope to receive guidance from advanced opinions to improve.

Lawyers Visiting Inmates at Ward Road Prison: Regulations 113

Limited to Members of the Bar Association

When lawyers go to visit inmates at the Ward Road Prison in Shanghai, the prison staff uses the membership list of the Bar Association as the standard. Only those who are on the membership list are allowed to visit. Recently, Lawyer Jia Yaoxi was entrusted by his client to visit an inmate at the prison the other day. Because Lawyer Jia had only joined the association last month and was not yet added to the membership list, he was refused by the prison. Lawyer Jia then presented his lawyer badge, but the prison staff refused to allow him to visit, resulting in a wasted trip. Afterwards, Lawyer Jia sent a letter to the Standing Committee of the Shanghai Bar Association, requesting that they quickly forward a letter of certification to the prison management staff before he could visit the inmates again.

Continued Report on Lottery Ticket Drawing Method 122

The detailed method for drawing the National Government Aviation Highway Construction Lottery Tickets has been reported in this newspaper. According to our investigation, during the 25th joint meeting of the lottery ticket committee on the 31st of last month, Director Chen of the lottery ticket office made an important proposal regarding the drawing: "It has been found that the ticket number balls used for drawing are three thousand four-digit balls, from 0000 to 2999, and one hundred two-digit balls, from 00 to 99. Therefore, the numbers that can be drawn range from a minimum of 000000 to a maximum of 299999. In fact, 300000 cannot be drawn. However, the numbers of the issued lottery tickets range from 000001 to 300000. In order to maintain the integrity of the numbers, it is proposed to stipulate that ticket number ball number 000000 be used to replace 300000. If 000000 is drawn, it means number 300000 in the lottery tickets has won. Also, the newly revised prize level table lists bonus prizes, such as first and second prizes being the smallest or largest number, and the associated upper and lower numbers for bonus prizes. It is proposed to use a circular method to determine them. For example, if the first prize number drawn is 000000, i.e., 3(00000), then lottery ticket numbers 299999 and 000001 will be its upper and lower associated bonus prizes. If the first prize is number 000001, then its bonus prizes will be number 300000 and number 000002. Is this feasible? Please decide publicly." The committee, considering that this matter concerns the integrity of the ball ticket numbers and solves the problem of associated bonus prize numbers, passed the proposal and decided to implement it starting from the 13th drawing (August 9th).

Reasons for Rising Flower Cloth Prices 125

According to Xinxin News Agency, the price of flower cloth has been rising recently. The reason is that a certain party has jointly formed a company to borrow money to purchase goods, trying to artificially raise flower prices in order to profit from it. Therefore, they mostly adopt a policy of reducing loans for those who pledge old flowers. It is said that an agreement is already in sight.

Three Perpetrators of Assault Sentenced to Eight Months Each 129

Wang Jinrong, a worker from Yufeng Yarn Factory, from Dongtai, had a minor disagreement with a certain Qu from Qin Prefecture in the same factory at about 4:00 PM on the 23rd of last month. Xu Peikun Discusses Recent Developments in the Financial Industry 130

Recently, the financial situation in Shanghai has been chaotic. Our reporter specially interviewed economic expert Mr. Xu Peikun, questioning him about everything. His comments are revealed below:

In the past two weeks, rumors have flourished in Shanghai, and the financial market has been unusually chaotic. Margin calls and foreign exchange rates have soared and plummeted wildly. If this continues, not only will individuals be affected, but the national finances will inevitably fall into a desperate situation. Everyone knows that our country's economic structure is not sound. If we do not cultivate it to consolidate its foundation, the consequences are self-evident. Based on the situation in the past two weeks, the trend is extremely frightening. Everyone feels insecure and cannot rest easy. Those with assets are either rushing to buy spot goods for hoarding or buying up foreign exchange bills to seek safety. The more capital that escapes, the more the domestic financial system will be depleted, and the market will become increasingly chaotic and deteriorate. Agriculture, industry, and commerce will have no hope of recovery. The recent tension and panic are all due to rumors, especially regarding inflation. It is as if the government will implement inflation, making all money useless, and all industries hopeless. People are rushing to escape while they still have a breath left. It's like "one dog barks at a shadow, and a hundred dogs bark along." In an instant, it turns into a citywide panic.

However, we clearly know that the government will not implement an inflationary policy at this time. The recent rise in public prices is a very obvious indication. Moreover, the reserves of both Chinese and foreign banks have increased. For example, in 1929, it was 240,260,000 yuan; in 1930, it was 261,956,000 yuan; in 1931, it was 66,188,000 yuan; in 1932, it was 438,339,000 yuan; in 1933, it was 547,446,000 yuan; in 1934, it was 324,199,000 yuan; and in May 1935, it was 340,943,000 yuan. Except for the special circumstances of 1932 and 1933, the recent increase in reserves is very significant. If we only consider the reserves of Chinese banks, this year's reserves are higher than in any other year (except last year). That is, 290,165,000 yuan in May of this year, compared to the peak of 337,632,000 yuan in June of last year, the difference is very small. Moreover, this is due to the fact that all the silver in the interior is being imported into Shanghai. It can be seen that the outflow of silver is entirely silver from foreign banks. We cannot control its departure or retention. However, the amount of silver held by Chinese people is increasing endlessly. From this, it can be seen that the illness of today's market is not a lack of money but a lack of money circulation. It is like a person's illness is not anemia but polycythemia, making them prone to stroke.

In terms of the current market situation, the government has absolutely no need for inflation. If we consider the needs of large-scale economic construction across the country, there is a significant shortage of capital in all countries, which is indeed a symptom of anemia. However, inflation is definitely not the solution. Moreover, inflation is a very dangerous experiment, which I believe no wise financial authorities would be willing to undertake rashly. Perhaps the recent central government's plan to implement unified currency issuance has been mistaken for inflation, which is also possible. In fact, they are as different as heaven and earth. How can they be confused? The financial crisis that occurs every five years was fortunately quelled by the authorities' statement. Although the recent crisis was caused by unfounded rumors, the frightened birds urgently need a place to roost. Moreover, the matter is of great importance to the national economy and the people's livelihood, as mentioned above. The financial authorities are expected to pay attention to it. If a timely statement is made to correct the errors of the rumors, then the stability of the people's hearts can be expected immediately.

Furthermore, the subsidiary currency is complex and chaotic and must be reformed. However, if we only think that adopting the decimal system or using nickel to mint coins can solve the subsidiary currency problem, then we are missing the mark. Adopting the decimal system does have its conveniences, and it is extremely simple in terms of calculation. However, not adopting the decimal system or continuing to use the current subsidiary currency system is also not a hindrance. For example, the United Kingdom does not use the decimal system. Moreover, the lives of most people in our country are calculated in copper coins. Copper coins are to most people as silver dollars are to a few people. The reform of silver dollars can have a huge impact immediately, and the reform of copper coins will inevitably have an even greater impact. This subsidiary currency has been used for a long time, and the connection to people's livelihoods is extremely deep. In terms of the current state of people's livelihoods, there is no need for this reform.

Using nickel to mint subsidiary currency is even more ill-advised. In various countries in Europe and America, many of the smallest unit subsidiary currencies are minted with nickel. However, our country produces very little nickel. The smallest unit subsidiary currency is the copper coin and one-tenth of each copper coin. Using nickel would be even more uneconomical and would inevitably raise the standard of living suddenly, making it even more difficult for the common people to make a living. In short, there is no need to reform our country's smallest unit subsidiary currency, the copper coin, at present. Even for other subsidiary currencies, although there is no need for the decimal system, due to the issuance of silver dollar fractional notes, they are already trending towards the decimal system. The current subsidiary currency system has no fundamental flaws. The main reasons for the complexity and chaos are the lack of uniformity in the minting of subsidiary currency and the prevalence of private minting. If the central government can solve these two points satisfactorily, then the exchange rate between fractional silver dollars and the standard currency and the exchange rate between copper coins and the standard currency can be stabilized. Although there is no decimal system in name, there is the effect of the decimal system in reality. If the government wants to mint subsidiary currencies in units of fifty cents, twenty-five cents, or five cents, but lacks silver to mint them, then it may as well use antimony or tungsten to mint smaller unit coins, such as ten cents and five cents. This would not only promote domestic production but also increase chips, which seems to be slightly better than using nickel.

In conclusion, our country's subsidiary currency system is a currency system that is suitable for the living standards of the people. The areas that need reform are unifying the national subsidiary currency minting rights and cracking down on private minting. Other than that, it is not a matter of urgency. It is like dressing a weak body in fancy clothes, which is not beautiful and has no use. Recently, scholars have gradually begun to pay attention to production and sales issues, which is a good phenomenon. The root of our country's economic problems lies in the irrationality of production and sales and the irrationality of business management. The former can be seen in the issue of food. Although we claim to be a country based on agriculture, we have to rely on foreign rice and wheat. What else can we say? Mr. Peng Xuepei's advocacy of a policy of food self-sufficiency is indeed a life-saving policy. The latter can be seen in adherence to old customs. The management methods of our country's agriculture, industry, and commerce, except for a very small number of modernized enterprises, have not changed. However, the enterprises of other countries are changing with each passing day. How can we compete? The recent failures of financial businesses are also due to clinging to old habits. Minister Kong's explanation of the weaknesses of money shops is also nothing more than wanting to encourage the business community to work hard to move forward and achieve self-reliance.

In the above, it is said that our country's finances have not deteriorated and that there should be no difficulties in turnover since there are many reserves. However, what is frightening is that the impact of instability has created vigilance, and people are afraid to invest. At the same time, on the government side, the progress of construction projects, such as the construction of highways and waterways, and the establishment of various weighing factories, require a lot of money, which the reserves of Shanghai alone cannot cope with. This extra funding must be raised separately. In this turbulent time, people are panicking. It is appropriate to be open and honest and cooperate between the government and the public. For any new facilities, the government should carefully study them to establish trust and show impartiality. Mr. Kong has adopted the principles of stabilizing finance and stabilizing people's hearts. The current need is nothing more than seeking a strategy to stabilize the situation.

French Concession Police Continue to Arrest Rickshaws Yesterday 131

The total number has exceeded a thousand, and the situation is very serious. Rickshaw pullers petition party and government agencies for prompt negotiation.

According to the New Voice News Agency, rickshaw pullers in the French Concession do not support the Municipal Council's registration of rickshaw pullers. Therefore, the bureau began registration for a month, but no one applied. It was then stipulated that registration would be compulsory from August 1. Otherwise, vehicles would be detained, and they would only be returned after the rickshaw puller had registered. However, the rickshaw pullers still ignored the bureau's announcement. Therefore, 700 vehicles were detained on the 1st. Yesterday, the police continued to arrest them. Including the previous day, the number has exceeded a thousand, and they are being detained in various police stations.

Compulsory Registration

When the police arrest vehicles, most rickshaw pullers abandon their vehicles and flee. However, the police's initial intention was to force rickshaw pullers to register. Therefore, when arresting vehicles, they also arrested rickshaw pullers and took them to the registration office on Route Ghisi to register. In the past two days, only 14 rickshaw pullers were forced to register (there are more than 40,300 rickshaw pullers and 7,100 rickshaws in the French Concession).

Reduced Number of Vehicles

Since more than a thousand vehicles were detained by the police, the number of rickshaws in the French Concession has decreased. Usually, at the intersections of the two concessions, there are vehicles with "small permits" (i.e., French Concession permits) parked on the road. Now, because of the police arrests, rickshaw pullers dare not stop. As a result, fares have also doubled, causing hardship for pedestrians. The business of trams and buses has flourished as a result.

Report to the Chamber of Commerce

Rickshaw pullers are unable to operate due to the detention of their vehicles, causing extreme panic in their livelihoods. They are all bringing their families and children to complain to the owners and the trade association. The rickshaw industry trade association specially sent representatives Qiu Chunshan, Yu Dajin, Zhou Jinyuan, and others to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday to report the situation and ask for justice to be upheld and the actions of the French Concession to be corrected. The association's secretary, Yan Esheng, met with them and promised to send someone to investigate and handle the matter thoroughly.

Representatives Petition

Based on the resolution of the general meeting, representatives of the rickshaw pullers in the French Concession, including Xu Hongsheng, Zhou Li, Lü Yigao, Zhou Yongcai, Li Asi, and Yang Yougui, went to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau at 2:00 PM yesterday with a written petition. The bureau stated that the petition was not stamped and did not meet the formal requirements of official documents. Therefore, they were asked to complete the procedures and wait for review. They then went to the Municipal Government, but it was past office hours. Therefore, it was decided to go again at 9:00 AM today. At the same time, it was also decided to petition the Chinese Ratepayers' Association of the French Concession, the Citizens' Federation, and various organizations for assistance.

Submit Documents to the Party and Government

The rickshaw pullers submitted documents to various party and government agencies, stating: "Regarding the petition, the French Concession in this city is conducting a registration for public rickshaws. Since the announcement, the rickshaw pullers have been repeatedly advised by the trade association to proceed. However, the general coolie rickshaw pullers have been hesitant to move forward. This is because rickshaw pullers have many individual sufferings and sufferings associated with the rickshaw owners. We respectfully submit the details of the treatment in the concession: Rickshaw pulling is a profession where people work like animals, regardless of cold or heat, and rushing about without leisure. After paying the rickshaw owner's rent every day, the meager earnings are barely enough to fill their stomachs. If there are slightly more people in the family, they often have to endure hunger and starvation. It is even more common that business is slow and the earnings are not enough to pay the rent, resulting in days without food. Now, rickshaw pullers are required to register, and each person must pay a fee of fifty cents. This is rickshaw pullers' individual suffering number one. French Concession police need to fulfill a certain number of official duties every month. Therefore, rickshaw permits are often confiscated for no reason, and permits are lost or stolen. It is not possible to reissue them at any time, resulting in the suspension of vehicles. This is the rickshaw pullers' and rickshaw owners' joint suffering number two. According to human principles, even if they register, they should not be photographed or fingerprinted. Such behavior insults the rickshaw pullers' reputation and the rickshaw pullers' personality, reaching the extreme. This is rickshaw pullers' individual suffering number three. Moreover, rickshaw pullers take advantage of the busy farming season in the countryside to come and go at will. Or they have no fixed property or residence to rely on. They make a living by pulling rickshaws, coming and going freely, and there is no possibility of restriction. This is rickshaw pullers' individual suffering number four. In summary, the above points are illegal acts. Moreover, they are oppressing rickshaw pullers with harsh measures. Yesterday alone, hundreds of vehicles were detained. It is clearly seen that they are deliberately making things difficult for rickshaw pullers. At a time when the city is sluggish and various industries are struggling, the authorities should be providing relief. How can they allow the concession to recklessly exploit them? The public sentiment among rickshaw pullers is surging and unstoppable. Once a major disaster occurs, how can the overall situation be imagined? Therefore, we submit this petition, requesting your department (bureau) to show compassion for our suffering, and approve the transfer to the relevant authorities to carefully consider and allow the above points to be granted. Regarding the registration, or there may be room for maneuver. Otherwise, it is difficult to approve. We present this petition with extreme trepidation, awaiting your orders."

Rickshaw Business Statement

The Rickshaw Association issued a statement regarding the issue of responsibility: "The French Concession's current registration of public rickshaw pullers has caused all rickshaw pullers to express their opposition due to their own interests. In order to maintain their business, rickshaw owners sympathize with the rickshaw pullers. This association is the only legal group of rickshaw owners in this city, and it is our duty to safeguard the business of rickshaw owners. We have no hesitation in representing the public opinion of rickshaw owners, running around for negotiations, and appealing for assistance. Thanks to the Social Affairs Bureau and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for coming forward to mediate. On the rickshaw owner's side, for the sake of social security, we have always respected the opinions of the mediators and waited quietly for a solution. However, the French Concession authorities insisted on their established methods and refused to listen to others. As a result, all mediation efforts were ineffective. Moreover, the French Concession police stations took decisive measures from August 1, forcing rickshaw pullers to register and arresting vehicles along the way, detaining them in police stations. The number of arrested vehicles has reached several hundred. The losses suffered by rickshaw owners are extremely deep and significant. The number of rickshaw pullers forced to lose their jobs is nearly a thousand. Their livelihoods are cut off, and the public is in constant panic. In view of the ineffectiveness of mediation and the exhaustion of all negotiations, and the increasing number of vehicles forced to suspend operations and the unemployed rickshaw puller masses, if an unexpected dispute is triggered, the responsibility should be borne by those who caused this incident. In addition to protecting the business of rickshaw owners in accordance with the law, this association will not be involved in any actions taken by rickshaw owners and rickshaw pullers. We are afraid that the public may not understand the truth, so we hereby declare this."

Pawnshops in This City Submitted a Petition to the Social Affairs Bureau Yesterday 132

Reporting the history and current situation of the industry, which is affected by the market and has undergone great changes.

The Shanghai Pawnshop Trade Association previously received instructions from the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau to conduct a thorough investigation of the industry and report it to the bureau for relief purposes. After receiving the order, the association has now completed the investigation and mailed it to the bureau for review yesterday afternoon. The original petition and statement of the actual situation of the industry are as follows:

Document Submitted to the Social Affairs Bureau

Regarding the submission of a report, in accordance with Order No. 6293 of the Municipal Bureau dated July 24, which stated: "In order to provide relief to businesses, this bureau previously formulated a Shanghai business situation investigation form. In April of this year, all industry associations were instructed to conduct a thorough investigation according to the form, discuss and report it, and submit it to the bureau within one month. The association has been overdue for a long time. Therefore, this order instructs the association to promptly comply with the previous order and submit a detailed investigation report within fifteen days of receiving this document, without further delay or blame. This order is hereby issued." After receiving this, we immediately complied with the previously issued form and truthfully filled it out below. We respectfully request your review and approval, which would be a great benefit. Respectfully submitted to Wu, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau.

Evolution and Current Status

1. Changes and Overview of Business Operations Over the Years: Pawnshops are a convenient industry for the people. The internal organization and business operations have rarely changed throughout history. In times of thriving markets and social stability, they rely on interest income to cover various expenses. In addition to dividends, even if there are profits, they are very limited.

2. Recent Business Situation and Reasons for Its Decline: Since the January 28 Incident, the market has been sluggish, and prices have plummeted. Most customers abandon their pawned goods without redeeming them, resulting in a sharp decline in interest income. Various expenses cannot be covered by revenue. The selling price of expired goods is only 60-70% of the pawned value. The loss of capital is truly significant. Therefore, those with weak financial resources have no choice but to close down. (1) Procurement and Manufacturing: The goods procured by pawnshops are all received through pawning. They do not engage in any manufacturing themselves. (2) Sales Situation: Expired pawned goods are usually returned to the pawnshop, which then purchases them at market value based on the expired pawn ticket. In times of thriving markets, the selling price can be 10-20% higher than the pawned value. Now, the market is declining, and buyers can inspect the goods item by item, which is called "looking at the goods." The value discussed by the buyer is only 60-70% of the pawned value. In order to sell the goods and seek profit, pawnshops have no choice but to sell them at a painful loss. (3) Comparison of Price Increases and Decreases Over the Years or Recently and the Main Reasons: Pawnshops accept daily necessities pawned by ordinary people. In times of stable prices, even after long-term storage for a year and a half, the capital can often be maintained when selling. However, nowadays, the styles of men's and women's clothing change rapidly, and prices continue to plummet. Many customers abandon their goods without redeeming them. When selling expired goods, they have to lose 30-40% compared to the pawned value. Compared with the past, the selling price is only half of what it used to be. For example, if the pawned value of a certain item is ten yuan, it can be sold for eleven or twelve yuan when it expires in a thriving market. Now, it can only be sold for six yuan. (4) Competition Between This Industry and Foreign Goods: Pawnshops are neither producers nor retailers, so there is no competition with other industries. (5) Difficulties in the Industry and Relief or Improvement Measures: The most difficult problem for pawnshops is that the operating income is not enough to cover expenses, the selling price of expired goods is repeatedly losing money, and the increased burden from employees' demands (although not fully implemented, the impact is very significant). At this time of market decline and financial drought, pawnshops feel the above difficulties very seriously. If this continues, they will all be forced to close down. If they want to provide relief, they must reduce rent, shorten the expiration date, lower the pawned value, and obtain low-interest funds for turnover to be effective. (6) Total Number of Employees and Treatment in This Industry: According to statistics from more than 30 pawnshops in the association, there are more than 500 employees in total. During the service period, in addition to salaries, there are also usage fees, which are distributed according to their duties. (7) Names of Newly Opened, Reorganized, and Closed Stores in Recent Years and the Reasons: In recent years, more than 20 pawnshops in the inland and concessions have closed down. The reason is that their businesses are declining and they are losing money. (8) Recent List of Store Names in This Industry That Have Joined and Have Not Joined the Association (Names and Addresses): Those who have joined the association are all stores opened in the inland. Their names and addresses have been reported to your bureau and are omitted here. Most of those who have not joined the association are stores in the concessions, so they cannot be reported.

Detained by the captain and sent to the police

At 10:30 AM yesterday, a self-owned car of the Bank of Communications, license plate number 10078, was transporting funds on Jinling Road, from Machen Road to Jinling Road. It was rented from the Feili Car Rental Company at 383 Xiaoshadu Road, which is under the jurisdiction of the Gordon Road Police Station. The city license number is 4313, and the rental license number is 17893. At the same time, opposite electric pole number 20, a small cart full of old long bamboo was parked. Seeing the Bank of Communications car approaching, the small cart deliberately blocked the road in the middle. At this time, the bandit car opposite electric pole number 19 rushed over and four people jumped out. Three of them were wearing blue cloth shirts and pants, and one bandit was wearing a Xiangyun gauze short shirt and pants. According to the accountant Liu Xilong, four people came to rent the car at the time. He then sent driver Liu Defa to drive the car. According to Liu Defa, he was sent by the accountant Mr. Liu to drive the car to the bottom of the Zhaofeng Garden at Datong University. The area was deserted. The bandits then pushed him out and were watched over by two people in the soybean field. They were released a short time later. As of the reporter's deadline, the car from the Feili Car Rental Company had not been found. The small cart with old long bamboo used in the robbery on Jinling Road was also detained, but the cart driver was not the actual perpetrator. According to the Hengfeng Road Police Station, the bandits were carrying four Mauser pistols. However, according to the investigation of passersby, there were two Mauser pistols and two handguns.

Homicide Resulting from Argument Over Borrowed Hairdressing Scissors; Verdict Rendered 135

Li Guangtai Sentenced to Two Years

Li Guangtai, a 17-year-old apprentice from Yangzhou working at the Gui Ji barbershop located at 198 Route Tenant de la Tour in the French Concession, had an argument with Rong Zhengbang, a 24-year-old fellow barber from Yangzhou, on July 8. Rong borrowed a pair of hairdressing scissors from Li, and after using them, he returned them without sharpening them. After closing shop at around 12:00 AM that night, the two argued and quarreled over the unsharpened scissors. Rong then became violent and beat Li. In desperation, Li, unable to resist, took the scissors and stabbed Rong once in the left rib, penetrating his lung. Rong fell to the ground after being injured. Fellow shop workers sent Rong to the hospital for treatment. The hospital, as per usual protocol, reported the incident to the police station. Detectives arrested the suspect, Li Guangtai, and took him to the First Special District Court for interrogation and investigation. Rong died on the 10th due to the severity of his injuries. The French police sent the body to the mortuary for examination. The Second Special District Court dispatched personnel to confirm the cause of death. The body was claimed by the family for burial. The French Police Department filed a public prosecution against Li for homicide. The details have been reported previously. The case has been investigated by Judge Sun Peng, and the date for the verdict was scheduled. Yesterday was the scheduled date for the verdict. Judge Li Changnian presided over the First Criminal Court on behalf of Judge Sun Peng. Li Guangtai was ordered to appear in court. After a brief interrogation of his age and background, the verdict was announced: Li Guangtai is sentenced to two years of imprisonment for causing death by injury. The number of days spent in detention prior to the judgment will be deducted from the prison sentence at a rate of one day of detention for one day of imprisonment. During the appeal period, the defendant will be transferred to the detention center to await instructions.

The Rampage of Wharf Bandits 136

Fish Lost, Knife Wielded A Lone Bandit

Yu, a fishmonger from Pudong named Yan A, is forty-four years old this year. His home is at the Jialukou (i.e., Longzhen) in Pudong. As usual, he would come to Shanghai at midnight to wholesale fish at the 16th Pier Fish Market, and then carry them back to Gongzhen to sell in the morning, which he did every day. The day before yesterday at midnight, Yan shouldered a carrying basket and came to Shanghai via the Bo Wharf, arriving at the fish market pier outside the 16th Pier of the French Concession (i.e., the Iced Fresh Wharf), waiting for the fishing boats to arrive and wholesale fish. Because it was still early, Yan sat on the pier to cool off and doze. In a short while, he was fast asleep. At one o'clock yesterday morning, suddenly three wharf bandits came together and, taking advantage of Yan's sleep, tried to reach into Yan's stomach pocket to steal silver coins. Yan woke up in shock in his dream, and saw that the three bandits were still trying to forcefully snatch it. Yan shouted, "Robbers!" One of the three bandits immediately took out a sharp knife and stabbed Yan's lips and left and right arms five or six times, causing blood to flow. The bandits then released their hold and fled. Yan still tried to stand up to pursue them, but fell to the ground in pain. One of the patrols, No. 156, and No. 542, a Chinese patrolman, heard the alarm and rushed over, capturing one bandit. He confessed his name was Zhou Chunsheng, eighteen years old, from Jiangbei, and lived at No. 13, Jinda Lane, Lan Ni Du, Pudong. He admitted that because the theft was unsuccessful, he committed the assault out of spite. His accomplices, Wang Atang and Li Jinbiao, had already escaped. The patrolman immediately took Zhou to the Xiaodongmen French Police Station for detention pending investigation. On one hand, the patrol head dispatched Detective Xu Guilin to send the injured person to the hospital for treatment. It is said that the injury was quite serious. At ten o'clock yesterday morning, the police station escorted the bandit Zhou to the Criminal First Tribunal of the Second Special Court, where Judge Li Changnian conducted the trial. Attorney Yuan Jiahuang of the Police Department presented the case, stating that the police station had not yet completed the investigation and needed to apprehend the remaining accomplices. The victim was also still in the hospital receiving treatment and had not yet recovered. He requested that the hearing be postponed. The court verified the report, interrogated the defendant Zhou Chunsheng, and then ordered that the hearing be postponed for seven days. The defendant was remanded in custody.

After Chen Liana Committed Suicide by Poison, Her Mother and Son-in-Law Are in Litigation 138

Disputes Once Arose over Jewelry Why Was the Injury Report Submitted After Death?

Zheng Yugui, the young owner of the Yongning Pawnshop at No. 20 Chengdu Road, is from Chaoyang, Guangdong. He is currently nineteen years old and still studying. When Zheng was four years old, he was betrothed by his parents to Chen Liana (one year older than Zheng Yugui), the daughter of Chen Xiushan, a Teochew merchant in Shanghai. By the winter before last, because both the man and woman had grown up, they held a wedding on October 21st of that year. On the morning of the 9th of last month, at around 11:00 AM, Chen Liana suddenly committed suicide by opium. The police were notified, and she was taken to the hospital by car.

Treatment was Ineffective

She died at 1:00 AM on the 10th. The prosecutor of the First Special District Court examined the body and confirmed that she had died by suicide. He ordered the body to be taken away for burial. After his wife's death, Zheng Yugui discovered that about 10,000 yuan worth of his wife's jewelry was missing. He reported to the Chengdu Road Police Station and requested an investigation. On the 17th of last month, Zheng found two notes left by Chen Liana in a drawer. One note said:

All jewelry

Is placed in the rattan basket in the third-floor bathroom of my mother's house. The other note said that after death, she must be dressed in He Xian's clothes. These clothes were also in the rattan basket. When Zheng saw these two notes, he noted that the clothes that the deceased wore when she was encoffined were all brought by his in-laws, and they matched what was written on the notes. Therefore, there was no doubt that the jewelry was in his in-laws' house. He then reported the situation

To the police station

The police station ordered Chinese detective Huang Fusen and Western detective Harvey to go to Zheng's in-laws' house at No. 84, Yugu Village, Yuyuan Road, to investigate. According to Zheng's mother-in-law, Chen Yang, the bathroom had never been opened, and she did not know if the jewelry was there. She then claimed that the jewelry had been handed over to her son-in-law at the Wan Guo Funeral Home. At the time, Zheng thought that since they were relatives, it would be better to postpone the negotiation. However, the next day (the 18th), Chen Yang also reported to the Chengdu Road Police Station, saying that her

Son-in-Law Zheng Yugui

Had repeatedly abused her daughter. Before March 12th last year, he had beaten his daughter Liana, causing injuries. She was treated at Renji Hospital, and there was an injury report. The injury report was handed over to the maid, Lu Wu, before she committed suicide and then transferred to me. She requested that a public prosecution be initiated. On the one hand, Xu Hu hired lawyer Pan Zhensheng to write a complaint to the court, requesting that he be sentenced to imprisonment for not more than one year in accordance with Article 239 of the New Criminal Law for having a spouse and committing adultery with others, and the adulterer shall be punished in the same way. (It has been implemented since July 1st) According to Article 256 of the former Old Criminal Law, a married woman who commits adultery with others shall be sentenced to imprisonment for two years, and the adulterer shall be punished in the same way. This time, Ms. Xu Hu accused her husband of adultery, which is the first interesting case of its kind in the Local Court.

Hu Claimed that He Was Mentally Confused at the Time and Is Now Willing to Die to Repay His Wife's Life

Hu Shen, a woman from Shaoxing, 36 years old, recently rented a room alone at the home of Wang He, an old woman from the same hometown, at No. 464 Donghanbili Road. She worked at the Huaxing Tobacco Factory to support herself. Her husband, Hu Youxing, used to run a fresh meat shop, but has been unemployed for more than a year. Because he could not support his wife, they parted ways, and he stayed in Pudong. He thought that he had come to Shanghai from his hometown at noon on the 23rd of last month, and quarreled with Shen. She scolded him severely. Hu Youxing became angry and took a kitchen knife from the side and severely injured her head, causing blood to flow like a fountain. She fell to the ground and called for help. Chinese detective Zhang Youming and patrolman No. 1302 heard the alarm and came to arrest Hu. Together with the murder weapon, they were taken to the Huishan Police Station and sent to the First Special District Court. Because she was seriously injured in the hospital, she could not go to court to testify and was ordered to be remanded in custody, pending her recovery. However, Hu Shen died at 1:00 PM the next day. The body was sent to the Feilun Road Inspection Office, where the prosecutor appointed by the court examined the body and filed a case. Yesterday morning, Jiang Shuzi approved the case and presided over the trial in the Third Criminal Tribunal. Lawyer Wang Yaotang of the Public Works Department described what happened and said that Hu Shen was silent from the time she entered the hospital until her death. They did not know the truth of the serious matter that led to this tragedy. The deceased was usually very well-behaved, as confirmed by Ding Ren, a woman from the same factory. She said that she had worked with the deceased Hu Shen in the factory for a long time and had a very good character. My family lives at No. 101 Youheng Road. In the morning, she came to my place and asked me to eat watermelon. She didn't eat it and hurried back. Later, I learned that she was stabbed by her husband, but I didn't know the details. When asked, the defendant confessed that he married her when she was only 17 years old, but she was infertile. At that time, I went to ask her to wash my clothes, but she scolded me. In a moment of anger, I took a knife and stabbed her. The court declared that your wife's head was found to have knife wounds, and there were also bruises on her face and chest, which were purplish-blue, and blood was flowing from her eyes. Why did you do such a cruel thing? You might as well tell the truth. He replied that there was nothing else, and that he was mentally confused at the time and could not control himself. I am now willing to die to repay my wife's life, and so on. The judge appointed a lawyer to provide him with pro bono defense. He still was ordered to be remanded in custody, and a date was set for sentencing.

Revised English-Chinese Model Dictionary Published

Special Price: One Yuan Per Copy, Published by the Commercial Press

The English-Chinese Model Dictionary for Problem Solving and Composition, first published in 1929 by the Commercial Press, breaks away from the shortcomings of general English-Chinese dictionaries that translate European and American books. It pioneers a new path and takes a further step towards creative writing. In addition to explaining the meaning and pronunciation of words, it also demonstrates the usage of each word and its compounds in composition, combining the strengths of dictionaries for composition, rhetoric, conversation, and letter writing. It is an epoch-making work among English-Chinese dictionaries. Since its publication, students above middle school level and young people engaged in international trade have eagerly purchased and used it. Scholars have praised it unanimously, and Mr. Wu Zhihui even hailed it as the king of pocket dictionaries. Its academic value has long been established. Recently, the editors of the dictionary, recognizing that things have evolved and changed rapidly in recent years, and that new terms and meanings need to be supplemented, and that all parties value the book and hope it has the functions of a large dictionary, Zhang Shiliu and others formulated specific revision principles, consulted the latest Western books, and extensively revised the dictionary. In particular, all the features and new words of the Winoton Dictionary were adopted as much as possible. The number of single words has increased from 35,000 to over 40,000, and the number of compound words and example sentences has increased from 110,000 to over 120,000. The number of pages has increased from 1,400 to 1,700. In addition to the original four appendices, two new appendices, a phonetic person's name and place name table and an abbreviation table, have been added. The price of each copy has not been increased and remains at two yuan and five jiao, with a special price of only two yuan. It is available at all Commercial Press bookstores.
