Supplement to the Shanghai News

Talking Points

Another Modern Account 188

— Qiong Sheng

Last year, because it was the Year of Women's National Products, the Customs Office released alarming figures about the import of women's consumables, which caused many people to criticize women, believing that they were extravagant and unpatriotic. This year, the responsibility of the Year of National Products has shifted from women to students, so it naturally no longer attracts people's attention. However, we believe that the Year of National Products should not become a kind of play, with one act being performed and then another being switched out, with the aim of perfunctorily dealing with the present and deceiving the audience below the stage. Therefore, we don't mind being verbose and going against the ears of the "modern" misses and grandmothers, and talking about this matter again.

According to a conversation between the National Tariff Commission and reporters, "In the first half of this year alone, the import of women's consumables such as perfumes and cosmetics reached 558,770 national currency units, with no significant decrease compared to the same period last year. Among them, imports from the United States, Japan, and France were the most numerous, mostly consumed by the modern women of Shanghai," and so on. Naturally, this is only a small part of the spending on face and body. If the various clothes, jewelry, utensils, and so on are included in the statistics, the "alarming" figure would be more than this.

This figure is insignificant compared to the trade deficit of several hundred million yuan, but its seriousness lies in the fact that it is a non-productive expenditure. The large-scale import of these luxury consumables does not promote the domestic production industry, and shows that our women are now competing to be "modern." It cannot be denied that "love of beauty" is almost a human nature, but this "modern" trend contains countless evils and consequences. First, women's makeup and beauty lead to many things that are immoral and lose integrity, causing many romantic debts. The result is that women will inevitably suffer losses. Secondly, because of the influence of this "unrestrained extravagance of women," the entire society is also led into a situation of decadence and luxury. Naturally, "decadent ideas spread," and the result is the decline of social morals and the demise of people's will. Naturally, we do not stand on the side of the "defenders of the Way" to advocate "restoring old morality" or "changing customs," but in order to curb the growth of "servility" and to recover the determination and will to strive for independence and liberation, we are against this evil of women "forgetting reality."

For this reason, we have opened another general account of women's "modernity," hoping that women can receive some alarm, not just heartfelt words.

A Glimpse of Shi Qi 189

— Ai Tu

The night in the big cities of the South is rampant. The glamorous embankment, with its towering buildings, exudes a fascinating light, along with the dazzling street lights on the wharf. The crowds of people, the shouts of the coolies, form an uneasy night, and noisy sounds are moving and disturbing. At this moment, I, again with the traveler's absent-minded feeling, stepped into the cabin, letting it take me flying in the dark night of the sea, flowing downstream - the river surface at night is dark, like a devil opening its mouth wide, appearing unusually calm and desolate. Apart from hearing the unchanging sound of the river water rushing, there was also the sea breeze blowing from afar.

On the boat, I quickly fell asleep from exhaustion. The next day, when the gentle sun was smiling happily in the east, I was awakened by the noisy voices of a large group of travelers or sailors. I rubbed my eyes and ran to the deck to absorb the fresh morning sea breeze. At that time, when looking out with my eyes, I could see the reeds on both sides of the bank and the green forests on the plains, so charmingly dressed in the beautiful clothes of nature.

The boat passed through Bu Lan, and soon arrived at the prosperous Shi Qi. When the boat was still in the sea breeze, I could see the uneven wharves standing on the shore like rows of teeth, and various flags of different colors fluttering on the shore, beckoning. The uneven, old and new buildings followed the endless wharves, spreading far away. The desolate tower top on the high mountain in the city showed a terrible desolation and lonely sadness in the quiet morning. Among the city streets, there were occasionally large hotels standing tall, proudly flying the national flag - yes, they were the proud sons of heaven in the bustling markets of the countryside!

When the boat was docking at the not-so-clean wharf, before I even stepped ashore, many porters or rickshaw pullers blocked my way, shouting one sentence after another, unable to get out of the way:

"Hey! Sir! Go to ×× Hotel! It's half price there! Need a car?"

"Come, come! Here, I'll pull you there, I'll pull you there..."

The situation was really no different from that in big cities. From all aspects, one could see that there was deception and terrible evil hidden there. Those people with a cunning air gathered around me, like predators.

When wandering on the wide road, one could see from the crowded crowds everything that was no different from the big cities. The shop assistants were shouting with wide-open mouths at the entrances of the big shops, there were flags embroidered with flowers and advertising big discounts, there were bitter smiling faces, some showing extremely lively business, while others were so cold that even the shop assistants were dozing off. The gramophone melodies of the department stores were blasting so vigorously. The big hotels, as if afraid that people would not know how beautiful they were, were still displaying the touching patterns of business outside the threshold. Also, the fragrances exuding from the show windows of the large hotels, the fascinating music coming from the large theaters, the aloofness and solemnity of the large banks, all of these, coupled with the faces of the daughters of the metropolitan city covered with fragrant powder, the charming fashions, the graceful posture of high heels - all of these can represent the prosperity of Sun Yat-sen's hometown. The colors of progress have been constantly turning with the wheels of the times. Perhaps, this place can be considered a very outstanding market town! Even the "blind man's cake," "oyster sauce," and "seafood delicacies" produced here are quite famous.

The streets in the market towns of Guangdong are longitudinal, horizontal, or curved. When I ran until I was exhausted, I finally stepped onto the mountain peak and went to the Buddhist temple to absorb the fresh river breeze. At this time, one could even see the vigorous colors of a new town. The white buildings reflected against the white sky, and everywhere one could see black smoke rising from the black chimneys of small factories, spreading out into the sky in puffs.

Apart from some extravagant shadows, we can also see simple girls with healthy bodies walking on the streets - all of this makes people unable to forget that it (Shi Qi) is a new town with lush vitality, full of vivid and alluring shadows.

Sea Sickness 190

— Lao Xin

Before I even went to sea, I heard people say that people who are not healthy will get "seasick" when they go to sea. Seasickness, as the refined people say, is "sea sickness." That is to say, it is a disease that one gets only when one goes to sea. Once one leaves the sea, the disease will slowly get better without needing treatment. This disease originally has no borders; it is not as if foreigners will not get it. Moreover, the name of this sea sickness was even translated from foreigners. Sea sickness is originally a terrible and strange disease, but it only gives more opportunities to those who are not healthy: friends who are used to comfort suddenly come to this crazy sea, living the kind of unstable and upside-down life, of course they cannot get used to it. Therefore, they will have mental discomfort, leading to vomiting and dizziness. It is very reasonable. Because of this, even though my friends warned me in every way, I did not take it to heart, because I have never been someone who is used to living a comfortable life, and I have not lived at sea for a short time, although it is an inland river, but is it not the same? Therefore, although I am drifting on the sea alone this time, I am not afraid.

The ship slowly sailed out of the inland river and arrived on the coast of the boundless Pacific Ocean. Originally, the sea waves near the shore are much smaller than the sea waves when traversing the Pacific Ocean, but compared to the inland river, they are much bigger. Moreover, the time is also early autumn, the visible waves are not large, but the "ground swells" are very severe, that is, the reaction of the water. They are all rebelling inside the sea. Although there are no waves as high as the Himalayas throwing over on the surface, their silent reaction under the hull is even worse than the obvious waves. For the gentlemen who generally live in comfort and ease, this is undoubtedly a huge threat. Therefore, the sound of vomiting increases proportionally with the instability of the hull.

Perhaps it was out of schadenfreude, I took a great risk to walk from the steerage to those so-called cabins to see the ugliness of these civilized people. – “A wonder!” I saw many ladies like "little squirrels" and "little birds" lying their entire bodies on men, presenting a gray-white face like an anemic patient, their lips also white without a trace of blood, a long string of saliva hanging from their mouths, groaning like a dying patient. I was wondering in my heart, who would believe that the so-called charming "beauties" who enjoy themselves in the city, their faces painted red and white, are originally such a "skeleton."

I praised the sea, she is so fair, she is like an impartial judge, very different from the city that has changed its color after being influenced by money. Her rioting authority is a punishment for those who live in comfort. Therefore, I also thought that sea sickness has no boundaries. What it has first is a terrible test for people living in places without waves.

Thinking back to myself, it is good that I have not been troubled by this terrible test, because I am also a vagrant who lives an unstable life in the midst of waves. Being at sea or not being at sea is originally the same, living under terrible storms, with no difference. Therefore, although the sea is terrible, its raging waves are already a very common thing for us. Even so, I am still praising the sea, because its gift of raging waves can be considered a relatively fair one in the midst of unfairness.

However, there is no definite view of things in the world, especially in this kaleidoscope-like society. Or, in another person's view, such as that of gentlemen and ladies, perhaps their view of this kind of thing is exactly the opposite of ours. Not only do they not praise the sea, but they also curse "sea sickness" for its cruelty to them. Naturally, their or her opinions are all correct. In fact, what else can they feel about their own suffering other than that others or a third party are cruel! However, it cannot be said that my praise of the sea or my liking for "sea sickness" is wrong. Of course, I have my reasons, and my humble status in society can prove it.

Summer Evening (Part 1) 191

— Ya Fei

Colorful clouds are dancing in the distant cooking smoke. The faint sound of a shepherd's flute is passing through the nearby fields. On the mud road over there, three or five shepherd boys are lying on the backs of old oxen, slowly returning to the village, while the farmers, having finished weeding the rice in the fields, are dragging their tired bodies and walking home.

Women's shouts, men's conversations, children's cries, and goats' bellows are rippling in the village in waves. The entire village is full of noisy sounds, and the air suddenly seems irritable.

Those women have just helped their husbands weed the fields and returned, but they still cannot have a moment's rest. They are busy nursing their children, feeding the goats grass, fixing dinner, preparing bathwater for the men, and bathing the children… They are truly so busy that they cannot breathe. However, those who do not farm and have no children have already eaten dinner, taken a bath, changed clothes, and sat in the open space in front of the door, fanning themselves with palm-leaf fans to enjoy the cool breeze. Sometimes, when they are happy, they will hum those old-fashioned mountain songs. They see them being so busy, but are unconsciously proud of their own leisure. However, for them, they only often resent their fate:

"I'm busy like a busy person all year round, but I still often have to worry about going hungry. Unlike other people's comfortable lives, they eat well and dress well every day. They don't have to go up the mountain to chop firewood, and they don't have to go down to the fields to pull weeds! Alas! It's like we were born with a poor fate..." Sometimes when they hear the noise of the children or the bleating of the goats in the pen, it will further cause them annoyance and impatience: "Damned goats, little ghosts, are you all going to die soon?"

My house is completely dark and I don't even light a lamp. The mosquitoes have set up a Yellow River formation inside and outside the door. Mosquito-repellent smoke, which smells extremely unpleasant, is burning on the ground, and the smoke covers the entire house. Their formation is also somewhat chaotic: they are buzzing and flying around in the air, making a sound like a scattered bee hive. Qi Bang A Gen is lying on the edge of the courtyard, but has become the target of the mosquitoes' attack. He is waving a cattail fan to drive them away while slapping them with his hands, but they are still constantly sneaking attacks on every part of his body, every piece of his flesh!

"Dead mosquitoes, plague mosquitoes, I'm tired and want to sleep, but you all have to come find me." He finally grumbled and got up, walked to the back door and sat down on the small stone bridge under the Nanni fan-shelf. (To be continued)

Broadcasting News 197

Mr. Bao Mingshan, editor and publisher of the Chinese Harmonica Circle, teaches the performance of world-famous songs on the Huamei Radio Station (frequency 1060) every Sunday morning from 11:00 AM to 12:00 PM. It is heard that this Sunday (August 4th), Mr. Bao has invited Mr. Yu Yuxing, our country's only chromatic harmonica expert, to come to Huamei Radio Station to broadcast a special program on chromatic harmonica and short scale harmonica. (Please read tomorrow's column for detailed program). Mr. Yu is famous throughout the country and has many harmonica works published. He usually promotes the art of harmonica very hard, such as founding the joint harmonica team of various universities in Hangzhou, the Suzhou Da Wu Harmonica Association, etc. Mr. Yu does not usually perform lightly. This public broadcast is because of a deep friendship with Mr. Bao, which he could not refuse, so he exceptionally makes his first performance after coming to Shanghai. Readers of this newspaper are requested to pay attention to listening at that time, and don't miss this good opportunity.

Movie News

Lianhua's Contribution to Children's Year 198

Chinese children's education has not been popularized, and Chinese children's educational films are even more lacking. This can be said to be a huge loss for China and for all Chinese children.

Taking "Little Angel" as an educational film for children is most appropriate, but its more valuable aspect is that it has educational significance and is presented in an interesting, lively and vivid manner.

Using Wang Renmei, Lin Chuchu, Tang Tianxiu, and Li Junpan, these first-class actors, and using Wu Yonggang, a most promising director, to direct, can already prove the superiority of this drama. What is even more noteworthy is the new child star Ge Youye in this film. Xianhua specially invited him from Hong Kong to help make this drama a success. The new star Liu Qiong also

Page 23

has new development opportunities.

"Little Angel" can make the audience feel the noblest, truest, and most beautiful emotions of mankind. It can give the audience a kind of ultimate love and spiritual nourishment. Let us look forward to it!

Chinese Anecdotes 199

The male and female protagonists of "Water Country Spring and Autumn" are two major celebrities who are currently highly regarded (because the time has not yet arrived for the film's maturity, the names are temporarily not announced).

Wan Cangsu is wholeheartedly devoted to discovering new talents, so in "Water Country Spring and Autumn", in addition to the two male and female protagonists, Zhao Zhenni, Dai Yanwan, Liu Li, Chen Juanjuan and others are all new people.

Wan Cang has a naughty son who is ten years old this year, and is the little overlord of Luyang Village. He gathers a group of naughty children in the lane to play movie-making games, and he directs, shouting "Camera", "Cut" very loudly. Someone said: Like father, like son, this is certainly believable.

The colleagues of Zhonghua who are staying behind are relatively relaxed in their work, so in addition to playing table tennis for recreation, they have also been actively studying Peking opera tirelessly these days.

Miss Yan Qun from Beiping has now been hired as a Mandarin professor at the Zhonghua Company.

Miss Wei Fen, the daughter of Bu Wancang, who played the daughter of Li Minghui in the Yi Hua's "Woman" and was regarded as an extraordinary little angel, will also be "active" in "Water Country Spring and Autumn."

There are three special features of the script for "Water Country Spring and Autumn": (1) The subject matter is realistic and tragic, (2) The plot is stimulating and powerful, (3) The background is majestic and vast.

Hu Die's Sorrow 200

Hu Die in "Night Fragrance" is a flower-selling working woman. Whenever the lights come on, she carries her flower basket and appears at the entrances of some dance halls and bars. Because her will is weak and she cannot resist the temptation of vanity, she is soon seduced by Sun Min, a young master who often appears in places of wine, red lights and green lights, and becomes his plaything. After a long time, Sun Min gradually lost interest in Hu Die? At this time, she was pregnant, her boudoir was empty, and she sat up until dawn every night. In fact, at this time Sun Min had already found a new love. The blow of "unbearable memories" was already enough to hurt Hu Die, and Sun Min would abandon him even more. At this time, she didn't know where to go, and she had no face to see her old father and mother when she returned home, which made her understanding of life only deception and insult.

Working Diary of Dayu Island 201

Today is our most memorable day, because our work on Dayu Island has begun today.

We got up at four o'clock in the morning, gathered and set off. The large team marched mightily towards Dayu Island.

Shidao is about seven or eight li away from Dayu Island. There are no vehicles to ride there, so everyone had to run hard on their two legs! Everyone was very excited, and the steps were neat and the discipline was strict.

It was really good weather when we got out of the door. We walked and walked to our destination! Dayu Island. We rested in a fisherman's home, then organized props, makeup... Everyone started working, and we observed everything about them in more detail, and conducted further research on their life and actions.

It is really a uniquely flavored fisherman's home. The fishy and humid air made our breathing blocked.

After Tian Fang put on makeup, he chatted with the fishermen, and the fishermen actually treated him as a companion and joked with him.

We left the fisherman's house and went to the beach, and the work was troublesome enough. Because of the tide, the boats could not go into the water, so Director Wang also helped to tow them. Only then could the boat go into the water.

Fu Baolu shook the large case very quickly, which surprised the boatmen. Strange! He would be able to shake it in a few minutes.

The position of the camera was placed on a rock, with raging waves in front and deep ditches behind. If you are not careful, there is a danger of both people and machines being destroyed. On a rock further behind, stood a crowd of men and women watching, their eyes staring straight at the mysterious camera!

At the beginning of filming, another problem arose: when the boat rowed into the lens, the boatmen refused to drop anchor and stop, saying that there were hidden reefs below. When Director Wang was forced to have no choice, he jumped into the bottom of the sea, which was ten feet deep, and floated up after lying dormant for six or seven minutes, proving that the bottom of the sea was sandy. The boatmen were then relieved to drop the anchor. It is said that the seabed is indeed full of hidden reefs, and in order to film the scene, they had to deceive them. Fu Baolu, Chen Tianguo, and Tian Fang drove piles in the deep water. After the filming was over, Director Wang still went into the water to retrieve the anchor.

After that, the entire crew boarded the boat from the beach again to shoot a few beautiful seascapes and returning fishing boats in the distance. The wind and waves were very strong, the small boat was very unfree to move, and it was not easy to stabilize the angle of the lens, but the photographer Shen Yongshi struggled with the sea with an indomitable spirit, and victory ultimately belonged to us.

Little sister Fang Li is very smart and learned the fishermen's folk songs just a few days after arriving at Shidao.

Miss Liu Liying also had the courage to go to sea. (Tianyi Communication)

Publishing World 203

The Electric Sound Film Picture Sound Weekly, volume 4, issue 31, was published today. The content of this issue is even more exciting than before. The cover is a photo of Chen Yanyan swimming, which is printed in three-color fine printing, beautiful and clear. On the inside cover, there are also specially selected beach photos of Ye Qiuxin, Diao Banhua, Gu Lanjun, Gao Qianping, Li Zhuozhuo, etc. In terms of text, there are dozens of articles such as "Hu Die Surrounded for the First Time After Returning to the Country," "Yuan Muzhi's Peculiar Habit of Smelling Cigarettes," "Diao Banhua's Unrequited Love," and "Hu Die Denies Engagement." Each issue only sells for five cents of silver. Entertainment Weekly, issue 5, was published today. In this issue, in terms of text, there are hundreds of articles such as "Yu Dafu is in Love with a Prostitute Yin Di," "Tan Ying is Pregnant," "The Secret of Diao Banhua's Silk Fan," and "Li Zhuozhuo's Arrogance Before Respect Afterwards." In terms of copperplate pictures, there are bathing photos of Ye Qiuxin, Gu Lanjun, Li Zhuozhuo, etc. The bottom cover is a semi-nude photo of Diao Banhua after bathing. Each issue of this publication sells for five cents of silver, making it a particularly affordable publication in the publishing world. All major bookstores and newsstands are selling it.
